end

local SprintGUI = {}
local AnimationGUI;

local localPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
local UserInputService = game:GetService('UserInputService');

local S = {}
S.Stamina = 100
S.Sprinting = false

local character;
local humanoid;

local maxStamina = 100;

task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(0.05) do
		if S.Sprinting == false then
			if S.Stamina < maxStamina then
				S.Stamina = math.clamp(S.Stamina + 0.5, 0, maxStamina)
			end
		end;
	end
end)
UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(Input, processed)
	if Input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift and UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() == nil then
		if AnimationGUI.Animated then return; end;
		S.Sprinting = true
	end
end)
UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(Input)
	if Input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift and UserInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() == nil then
		S.Sprinting = false
	end
end)


function SprintGUI:Enable()
	sprintGUI.Enabled = true
end;

function SprintGUI:Disable()
	sprintGUI.Enabled = false
end;

function SprintGUI:CharacterAdded(char)
	if not char then return; end;

	if localPlayer:GetAttribute('X2Stamina') == true then 
		maxStamina = 165; 
		S.Stamina = 165;
	end;

	character = char;

	humanoid = character:WaitForChild('Humanoid');

	humanoid.Jumping:Connect(function()
		local newStamina = math.clamp(S.Stamina - 10, 0, maxStamina)
		S.Stamina = newStamina;
		if newStamina == 0 then
			humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping, false)
			task.delay(2, function()
				humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping, true)
			end)
		end
	end)
end;

function SprintGUI:Start()
	task.defer(function()
		while task.wait(0.1) do
			if not character or not humanoid then continue; end;

			if localPlayer:FindFirstChild('respawningValue') then
				humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0;
				continue;
			end;

			if (S.Sprinting == true) and not AnimationGUI.Animated and humanoid.SeatPart == nil then
				if S.Stamina > 0 then
					S.Stamina = S.Stamina - 1
					humanoid.WalkSpeed = 21
				else
					humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
				end
			else
				if not AnimationGUI.Animated then
					humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
				end;
			end;

			BottomRightGUI:SetCharacterBar('Stamina', S.Stamina, maxStamina);
		end;
	end);
end;

function SprintGUI:Init()
	AnimationGUI = self.Controllers.UI.AnimationGUI;
	BottomRightGUI = self.Controllers.UI.BottomRightGUI;
end;

return SprintGUI

-- Ambient Sound Controller
-- Khizzer
-- September 11, 2021



local AmbientSoundController = {}

local Functions;

--local DAY_SOUND = 'rbxassetid://9112757705'
--local NIGHT_SOUND = 'rbxassetid://9172435866';

local DAY_SOUND = 'rbxassetid://238385471';
local NIGHT_SOUND = 'rbxassetid://179507208';



local NetworkController;

local sound;

function AmbientSoundController:ResetAmbientSound()
    sound.Volume = 0.25
    local clockTime = game.Lighting.ClockTime;
    if (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2) then
        sound.SoundId = NIGHT_SOUND;
    else
        sound.SoundId = DAY_SOUND;
    end;
end;

function AmbientSoundController:DisableAmbientSound()
    sound.Volume = 0;
end;

function AmbientSoundController:Start()
    local clockTime = game.Lighting.ClockTime;
    if (clockTime > 17.5) or (clockTime < 6.2) then
        sound.SoundId = NIGHT_SOUND;
    else
        sound.SoundId = DAY_SOUND;
    end;

    NetworkController.Connect('AmbientSound', function(timeOfDay)
        if timeOfDay == 'Day' then
            sound.SoundId = DAY_SOUND;
        else
            sound.SoundId = NIGHT_SOUND;
        end;
    end)
end;

function AmbientSoundController:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Functions = self.Shared.Functions;
    sound = Functions:Create'Sound'{
        Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts;
        Name = 'AmbientNoise';
        Looped = true;
        SoundId = DAY_SOUND;
        Playing = true;
        Volume = 0.35
    }
end;


return AmbientSoundController

local BillboardController = {};

function BillboardController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('BillboardUpdate', function(uiPageLayout, index)
        if not uiPageLayout or not index then return; end;
        pcall(function()
            uiPageLayout:JumpTo(index);
        end)
    end)
end;

end;

return BillboardController;

--[[
    CountdownController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
-- Countdown Controller
-- Khizzer
-- December 29, 2022



local CountdownController = {}

if true then return {} end;

local Firework;

local newYearPrefabs = ReplicatedStorage.NewYearSystem;

local fireworkLocations = newYearPrefabs.FireworkLocations:GetChildren();

local FIREWORK_COUNT = 300;

function CountdownController:_startFireworks()
    for i = 1, FIREWORK_COUNT do
        local fireworkPos = fireworkLocations[math.random(1, #fireworkLocations)].Position;

        task.spawn(function()
            Firework:CreateFirework(fireworkPos);
        end)

        task.wait(math.random(0.5, 2))
    end;
end;

function CountdownController:Start()
    local countdownPart = newYearPrefabs.Countdown;
    countdownPart.Parent = workspace;

    local newYear = os.time({
        year = 2023,
        month = 1,
        day = 1,
        hour = 8,
        min = 0,
        sec = 0
    });

    while true do
        local currentTime = os.time();

        local timeUntilTarget = math.max(newYear - currentTime, 0);

        local days = math.floor((timeUntilTarget / 60 / 60 / 24) % (365 + 0.2425))
        local hours = math.floor((timeUntilTarget / 60 / 60) % 24)
        local minutes = math.floor((timeUntilTarget / 60) % 60)
        local seconds = math.floor(timeUntilTarget % 60)

        local timeString = string.format("%02d:%02d:%02d:%02d", days, hours, minutes, seconds);

        if timeUntilTarget <= 0 then
            timeString = "Happy New Year!";
            countdownPart.CountdownGUI.TitleLabel:Destroy();
            self:_startFireworks();
            break;
        end;

        countdownPart.CountdownGUI.CountdownLabel.Text = timeString;
        task.wait(1);
    end;
end;

function CountdownController:Init()
    Firework = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Firework')));
end;


return CountdownController

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/CountdownController_contents/Firework.lua ---

--[[
    Firework (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment → CountdownController
    Parent: CountdownController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- // Â© 2021, Eddy, All rights reserved. // --

-- // Main module for the fireworks

-- // Services
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local DebrisService = game:GetService("Debris")

-- // Variables
local Components = ReplicatedStorage.Components
local Particles = Components.Particles

local fireworks = {}

-- Create firework
function fireworks:CreateFirework(pos, sp, expTime)
	if not pos then warn("Position of firework not provided.") return end
	
	local explodeTime = expTime or math.random(2, 5)
	local speed = sp or 50
	
	local mainPart = Components.firework:Clone()
	local launchSound = mainPart.LaunchSound
	local launchParticles = mainPart.LaunchParticles
	mainPart.Parent = workspace.Terrain
	mainPart.Position = pos
	
	launchSound:Play()
	
	local BodyVel = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", mainPart)
	BodyVel.Velocity = (CFrame.Angles(math.pi/2,0,0)*CFrame.Angles((math.random()-.6)*.6,(math.random()-.6)*.6,0)).LookVector * speed --(mainPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0)).lookVector * speed
	
	task.wait(explodeTime)
	
	mainPart.Transparency = 1
	launchParticles.Enabled = false
	BodyVel.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	mainPart.Anchored = true
	
	FireworkEffects(mainPart)

	DebrisService:AddItem(mainPart, explodeTime + 3) -- clean up after
end

function FireworkEffects(part)
	if not part then return end
	
	for _, parti in ipairs(Particles:GetChildren()) do
		if parti:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
			local partiClone = parti:Clone()
			partiClone.Parent = part
			partiClone.Enabled = true
			spawn(function()
				wait(0.5)
				partiClone.Enabled = false
			end)
		end
	end
	
	local explodeSound = part:FindFirstChild("ExplodeSound")
	if explodeSound then
		explodeSound:Play()
	end
end

return fireworks

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/DoorBarrierController.lua ---

--[[
    DoorBarrierController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local Trove;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local function evaluate(doorBarrier, condition, trove)
    if typeof(condition) == 'table' then --If team based whitelist
        if condition[localPlayer.Team.Name] or condition[localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') or '_NIL'] then
            doorBarrier.CanCollide = false;
        else
            doorBarrier.CanCollide = true;
        end;
        if trove then
            trove:Add(localPlayer:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Team'):Connect(function()
                evaluate(doorBarrier, condition)
            end))
            trove:Add(localPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Division'):Connect(function()
                evaluate(doorBarrier, condition)
            end))
        end;
    elseif typeof(condition) == 'function' then --If function based whitelist
        local triggerReEval = function()
            evaluate(doorBarrier, condition, trove)
        end

        if condition(localPlayer, triggerReEval) then --if meets condition
            doorBarrier.CanCollide = false;
        else
            doorBarrier.CanCollide = true;
        end;
    end;
end;

local function SetupDoorBarrier(doorBarrier)
    if not doorBarrier then
        return;
    end;

    local trove = Trove.new();
    trove:AttachToInstance(doorBarrier);

    local doorBarrierConfig = doorBarrier:WaitForChild('DoorBarrierConfig', 10);

    task.wait(1);

    if not doorBarrierConfig then
        warn(`No DoorBarrierConfig in {doorBarrier:GetFullName()}`);
        return;
    end;

    local condition = require(doorBarrierConfig);

    if condition == nil then
        return warn(`No condition in {doorBarrierConfig:GetFullName()}`);
    end;

    evaluate(doorBarrier, condition, trove);
end;

local DoorBarrierController = {};

function DoorBarrierController:Start()
    for i, v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('DoorBarrier') do
        SetupDoorBarrier(v);
    end;

    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('DoorBarrier'):Connect(function(doorBarrier)
        SetupDoorBarrier(doorBarrier);
    end);
end;

function DoorBarrierController:Init()
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end;

return DoorBarrierController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/DoorController.lua ---

--[[
    DoorController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local NetworkController;
local ModelAnimation;

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local DoorController = {};

function DoorController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('Door', function(door, targetCFrame, soundID, speed)
        if speed then
            TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
        else
            TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);
        end;
        ModelAnimation.new(door, TWEEN_INFO, targetCFrame):Play();

        local sound = newInstance('Sound');
        sound.SoundId = soundID;
        sound.Parent = door:FindFirstChild("InteractionPart");
        sound:Play();
        sound.Ended:Wait();
        sound:Destroy();
    end);

    NetworkController.Connect('DoubleDoors', function(leftDoor, rightDoor, targetCFrameLeft, targetCFrameRight, soundID, speed)
        if speed then
            TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);
        else
            TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);
        end;

        if leftDoor.Parent:FindFirstChild('InteractionPart') then
            ModelAnimation.new(leftDoor, TWEEN_INFO, targetCFrameLeft):Play();
            ModelAnimation.new(rightDoor, TWEEN_INFO, targetCFrameRight):Play();

            local sound = newInstance('Sound');
            sound.SoundId = soundID;
            sound.Parent = leftDoor.Parent.InteractionPart;
            sound:Play();
            sound.Ended:Wait();
            sound:Destroy();
        end;
	end);

    local function setupGroupDoor(door)
        local DoorConfig = door:FindFirstChild('DoorConfig', true);
        if DoorConfig and DoorConfig:IsA("ModuleScript") then
            local interactionPart = door:FindFirstChild('InteractionPart', true);
            local configuration = require(DoorConfig);
            if configuration.GroupCondition then
                local cachedResult = configuration.GroupCondition(game.Players.LocalPlayer);
                local value = Instance.new('BoolValue');
                value.Parent = interactionPart;
                value.Name = '_CACHE';
                value.Value = cachedResult;
            else
                warn(`Group door {DoorConfig:GetFullName()} has no group condition.`)
            end
        end;
    end;

	for _,v in next, game.CollectionService:GetTagged('GroupDoor') do
        setupGroupDoor(v);
	end;

    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('GroupDoor'):Connect(function(door)
        setupGroupDoor(door);
    end);
end;

function DoorController:Init()
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ModelAnimation = self.Modules.ModelAnimation;
end;

return DoorController;

local NetworkController;
local ModelAnimation;

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(2.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);

local function GateAnimation(gate, targetCFrame)
    ModelAnimation.new(gate, TWEEN_INFO, targetCFrame):Play();
end;

local GateController = {};

function GateController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('SlidingGate', GateAnimation);

    NetworkController.Connect('BoomGate', GateAnimation);
end;

function GateController:Init()
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    ModelAnimation = self.Modules.ModelAnimation;
end;

return GateController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/OverheadSignController.lua ---

--[[
    OverheadSignController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
-- Overhead Sign Controller
-- Khizzer
-- January 1, 2023

local OverheadSignGUI;
local TeamController;
local Maid;
local MouseTarget;

local _maid;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local mouse = localPlayer:GetMouse();

local OverheadSignController = {}

function OverheadSignController:Start()
    TeamController.ListenForTeamChange({['Translink'] = true}, function(isOnTeam, _teamName)
        if isOnTeam then
            _maid = Maid.new(mouse.Move:Connect(function()
                local mouseTarget = MouseTarget.Get(125);
                if mouseTarget then
                    if CollectionService:HasTag(mouseTarget, 'OverheadSign') then
                        OverheadSignGUI:Enable(mouseTarget, mouse);
                        --Move frame, make visible
                    else
                        OverheadSignGUI:Disable();
                        --Hide it
                    end;
                else
                    OverheadSignGUI:Disable();
                    --Hide it
                end;
            end));
        else
            if _maid then
                _maid:DoCleaning();
            end;
        end;
    end)
end;

function OverheadSignController:Init()
    MouseTarget = self.Modules.MouseTarget;
    Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
    TeamController = self.Controllers.TeamController;
    OverheadSignGUI = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('OverheadSignGUI')));
end;

return OverheadSignController

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/OverheadSignController_contents/OverheadSignGUI.lua ---

--[[
    OverheadSignGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment → OverheadSignController
    Parent: OverheadSignController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Overhead SignGUI
-- Khizzer
-- January 1, 2023



local OverheadSignGUI = {}

local Maid;
local NetworkController;

local _maid;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local UserInputService = game:GetService('UserInputService')
local playergui = localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerGui', 10);

local GUI_INSET_Y = game:GetService('GuiService'):GetGuiInset().Y;

local overheadSignGUI = playergui:WaitForChild('OverheadSignGUI', 10);
local UIScale = overheadSignGUI:WaitForChild('UIScale', 10);
local mainFrame = overheadSignGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local leftImage = bodyFrame.LeftImage;
local rightImage = bodyFrame.RightImage;
local currentImage = bodyFrame.CurrentImage;

local signs = {
    YellowCross = 'rbxassetid://11996978187';
    RedCross = 'rbxassetid://11996991966';
    GreenArrow = 'rbxassetid://11996993694';
}

local carousel = {
    'YellowCross';
    'RedCross';
    'GreenArrow';
};

local ORDER = {
    'YellowCross';
    'RedCross';
    'GreenArrow';
};

table.freeze(ORDER);

function OverheadSignGUI:_shiftImages(direction: 'Left' | 'Right')
    local newCarousel = {};
    if direction == 'Left' then
        for i = 1, #carousel do
            local index = i + 1;
            if index > #carousel then
                index = 1;
            end;
            newCarousel[i] = carousel[index];
        end;
    elseif direction == 'Right' then
        for i = 1, #carousel do
            local index = i - 1;
            if index < 1 then
                index = #carousel;
            end;
            newCarousel[i] = carousel[index];
        end;
    end;

    carousel = newCarousel;

    leftImage.Image = signs[carousel[1]];
    rightImage.Image = signs[carousel[3]];
    currentImage.Image = signs[carousel[2]];
end;

function OverheadSignGUI:_setCarousel(currentImage: 'YellowCross' | 'RedCross' | 'GreenArrow')
    local index = table.find(ORDER, currentImage);
    
    local leftImage = ORDER[index - 1] or ORDER[#ORDER];
    local rightImage = ORDER[index + 1] or ORDER[1];

    local newCarousel = {leftImage, currentImage, rightImage};
    carousel = newCarousel;
end;

local lastTarget;

function OverheadSignGUI:Enable(mouseTarget, mouse)
    mainFrame.Position = UDim2.fromOffset((mouse.X / UIScale.Scale) + 17, (mouse.Y / UIScale.Scale) + GUI_INSET_Y);
    
    if lastTarget == mouseTarget then return end;

    lastTarget = mouseTarget;

    local surfaceGui = mouseTarget:FindFirstChild('OverheadSignGUI');
    local signImage = surfaceGui:FindFirstChild('SignImage');

    for i,v in next, signs do
        if v == signImage.Image then
            OverheadSignGUI:_setCarousel(i);
            break;
        end;
    end;

    overheadSignGUI.Enabled = true;

    leftImage.Image = signs[carousel[1]];
    rightImage.Image = signs[carousel[3]];
    currentImage.Image = signs[carousel[2]];
    

    if not _maid then
        _maid = Maid.new();
    end;

    _maid:GiveTask(UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessedEvent)
        if gameProcessedEvent then return end;

        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Q then
            OverheadSignGUI:_shiftImages('Left');
            NetworkController.Send('OverheadSign', mouseTarget, currentImage.Image);
        elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.E then
            OverheadSignGUI:_shiftImages('Right');
            NetworkController.Send('OverheadSign', mouseTarget, currentImage.Image);
        end;
    end))
end;

function OverheadSignGUI:Disable()
    overheadSignGUI.Enabled = false;

    lastTarget = nil;
    if not _maid then
        return;
    end;
    _maid:DoCleaning();
    _maid = nil;
end

function OverheadSignGUI:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
end;


return OverheadSignGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/PrisonCellController.lua ---

--[[
    PrisonCellController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
-- Prison Cell Controller
-- Khizzer
-- February 1, 2022



local PrisonCellController = {}
local ModelAnimation;
local NetworkController;

local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(2.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);


local function CellAnimation(cellName, targetCFrame, openedStatus)
    ModelAnimation.new(workspace.PrisonCells[cellName].Main, TWEEN_INFO, targetCFrame):Play();
    workspace.PrisonCells[cellName]:SetAttribute('Opened', openedStatus);
end;

local closedDoors = {};

function PrisonCellController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('PrisonCell', CellAnimation);

    for _,v in next, workspace.PrisonCells:GetChildren() do
        local opened = v:GetAttribute('Opened');

        if opened == false then
            closedDoors[v.Name] = true;
        end;
    end;

    workspace.PrisonCells:Destroy();
    ReplicatedStorage.PrisonCells:Clone().Parent = workspace;

    for _,v in next, workspace.PrisonCells:GetChildren() do
        local opened = v:GetAttribute('Opened');

        if closedDoors[v.Name] == true then
            v:SetAttribute('Opened', false);
            local door = v.Main;
            door:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(door.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-4.53, 0, 0));
        else
            v:SetAttribute('Opened', true);
        end;
    end;
end;

function PrisonCellController:Init()
    ModelAnimation = self.Modules.ModelAnimation;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end


return PrisonCellController

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/RotatingSignController.lua ---

--[[
    RotatingSignController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Rotating Sign Controller
-- Khizzer
-- August 23, 2021



local RotatingSignController = {Signs = {}}

local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local Streamable = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.Streamable.Streamable);

local Streamables = {};

function RotatingSignController:Start()
    for _,v in next, CollectionService:GetTagged('RotatingSign') do
        if not table.find(self.Signs, v) then
            if Streamables[v] then
                Streamables[v]:Destroy();
            end;

            local streamable = Streamable.primary(v);
            Streamables[v] = streamable;
            
            streamable:Observe(function(part, trove)
                self.Signs[#self.Signs + 1] = v;
                trove:Add(function()
                    for i,v2 in next, self.Signs do
                        if not v2.PrimaryPart then
                            table.remove(self.Signs, i)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end;
    end;

    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        for _,v in next, self.Signs do
            local _, isVisible = camera:WorldToScreenPoint(v.PrimaryPart.Position);
            if not isVisible then continue; end;
            local nextCFrame = v:GetPrimaryPartCFrame() * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesYXZ(0, v:FindFirstChild('Configuration').Speed.Value or 0.05, 0);
            v:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(nextCFrame);
        end;
    end)



    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('RotatingSign'):Connect(function(instance)
        if not table.find(self.Signs, instance) then
            if Streamables[instance] then
                Streamables[instance]:Destroy();
            end;

            local streamable = Streamable.primary(instance);
            Streamables[instance] = streamable;
            streamable:Observe(function(part, trove)
                self.Signs[#self.Signs + 1] = instance;
                trove:Add(function()
                    for i,v2 in next, self.Signs do
                        if not v2.PrimaryPart then
                            table.remove(self.Signs, i)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
        end;
    end)

    CollectionService:GetInstanceRemovedSignal('RotatingSign'):Connect(function(instance)
        local pos = table.find(self.Signs, instance);
        if pos then
            table.remove(self.Signs, pos);
        end
        if Streamables[instance] then
            Streamables[instance]:Destroy();
        end;
    end)
end;



return RotatingSignController

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Environment/WeatherController.lua ---

--[[
    WeatherController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Environment
    Parent: Environment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local WeatherController = {};

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local lighting = game:GetService('Lighting');
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');
local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local Rain;

local NetworkFunctionController

local stringSplit = string.split;

local RandomDecimal;
local NetworkController;

local AmbientSoundController;

local RAIN_SOUND = "rbxassetid://9142806929"
local SNOW_SOUND = 'rbxassetid://7921074965';

local thunderSoundsFolder = localPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild('Sounds', 10):WaitForChild('Thunder', 10);
local THUNDER_SOUNDS = thunderSoundsFolder:GetChildren();

type AtmosphereData = {
    Haze: number;
    Color: Color3;
    Density: number;
}

type RainData = {
    Enabled: boolean;
    IntensityRatio: number;
    StraightTexture: string?;
    TopDownTexture: string?;
};

type CloudData = {
    Density: number;
    Cover: number;
};

type WeatherData = {
    Atmosphere: AtmosphereData;
    Rain: RainData?;
    Clouds: CloudData;
    Probability: number
};

local Atmosphere: Atmosphere = lighting:WaitForChild('Atmosphere');
local Clouds: Clouds = workspace.Terrain:WaitForChild('Clouds')

local function SetRain(enabled)
    if enabled then
        Rain:SetStraightTexture("rbxassetid://1822883048");
        Rain:SetTopDownTexture("rbxassetid://1822856633");
        Rain:SetStraightSize(10);
        Rain:SetTopDownSize(NumberSequence.new {
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(0, 5.33, 2.75);
            NumberSequenceKeypoint.new(1, 5.33, 2.75);
        })
        Rain:SetSpeedRatio(1);
        Rain:SetDirection(Vector3.new(RandomDecimal(0, 0.5),-1,RandomDecimal(0, 0.5)));
        Rain:SetSoundId(RAIN_SOUND);
        Rain:SetCollisionMode(Rain.CollisionMode.Function, function(part)
            return not part:HasTag('RainIgnore')
        end)
        Rain:Enable();
    else
        AmbientSoundController:ResetAmbientSound()
        Rain:Disable();
    end;
end;

--[[ local function SetFog(value)
    AmbientSoundController:ResetAmbientSound();
    local data = stringSplit(value, ':');
    lighting.FogStart = data[1];
    lighting.FogEnd = data[2];
end; ]]

local function SetSnow(enabled)
    if enabled then
        AmbientSoundController:DisableAmbientSound();
        Rain:SetStraightTexture('rbxassetid://243664672');
        Rain:SetTopDownTexture('rbxassetid://243664672');
        --Rain:SetSplashTexture('rbxassetid://243664672');
        Rain:SetIntensityRatio(0.5);
        Rain:SetStraightSize(0.5);
        Rain:SetTopDownSize(0.5);
        Rain:SetSpeedRatio(0.3)
        Rain:SetVolume(0.3)
        Rain:Enable();
        Rain:SetDirection(Vector3.new(-0.75, -1, 0))
        Rain:SetSoundId(SNOW_SOUND)
    else
        AmbientSoundController:ResetAmbientSound();
        Rain:Disable()
    end;
end;

function WeatherController:Start()
    Rain:SetCollisionMode(Rain.CollisionMode.Blacklist, CollectionService:GetTagged('RainIgnore'));

    CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal('RainIgnore'):Connect(function()
        Rain:SetCollisionMode(Rain.CollisionMode.Blacklist, CollectionService:GetTagged('RainIgnore'));
    end)

    local oldWeather;
    local weatherTweens = {};

    --initial weather setup

    local initialWeather: WeatherData = NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GetInitialWeather');

    SetRain(initialWeather.Rain.Enabled);
    if initialWeather.Rain.IntensityRatio then
        Rain:SetIntensityRatio(initialWeather.Rain.IntensityRatio);
    end;

    if initialWeather.Rain.StraightTexture then
        Rain:SetStraightTexture(initialWeather.Rain.StraightTexture);
    end;
    if initialWeather.Rain.TopDownTexture then
        Rain:SetTopDownTexture(initialWeather.Rain.TopDownTexture);
    end;

    if initialWeather.Snow then
        SetSnow(true);
    end;

    Clouds.Density = initialWeather.Clouds.Density;
    Clouds.Cover = initialWeather.Clouds.Cover;

    Atmosphere.Haze = initialWeather.Atmosphere.Haze;
    Atmosphere.Density = initialWeather.Atmosphere.Density;
    -- Atmosphere.Color = initialWeather.Atmosphere.Color;

    oldWeather = initialWeather;


    NetworkController.Connect('onWeatherChange', function(weather: WeatherData, tweenTime: number)
        for _, tween in pairs(weatherTweens) do
            tween:Cancel();
            tween:Destroy();
        end;
        table.clear(weatherTweens);

        local atmosphereTween = TweenService:Create(Atmosphere, TweenInfo.new(tweenTime, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
            Haze = weather.Atmosphere.Haze;
            Density = weather.Atmosphere.Density;
            -- Color = weather.Atmosphere.Color;
        });

        table.insert(weatherTweens, atmosphereTween);

        local easingDirection = (weather.Rain.Enabled == true) and Enum.EasingDirection.In or Enum.EasingDirection.Out;
        local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(tweenTime, Enum.EasingStyle.Exponential, easingDirection);

        local cloudTween = TweenService:Create(Clouds, tweenInfo, {
            Density = weather.Clouds.Density;
            Cover = weather.Clouds.Cover;
        });

        table.insert(weatherTweens, cloudTween);

        if weather.Rain.Enabled == true and not weather.Snow then
            SetRain(true);
            local rainTween = Rain:SetTransparency(0, tweenInfo);
            table.insert(weatherTweens, rainTween);
        elseif oldWeather.Rain.Enabled == true and not weather.Snow then
            SetRain(false);
            local rainTween = Rain:SetTransparency(1, tweenInfo);
            table.insert(weatherTweens, rainTween);
        end;

        if weather.Snow then
            SetSnow(true);
            local snowTween = Rain:SetTransparency(0, tweenInfo);
            table.insert(weatherTweens, snowTween);
            if weather.Rain.IntensityRatio then
                Rain:SetIntensityRatio(weather.Rain.IntensityRatio);
            end;
        end

        for _,v in next, weatherTweens do
            v:Play();
        end;

        oldWeather = weather;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('Thunder', function()
        local function flashPropertyToWhite(property)
            task.defer(function()
                local initialValue = lighting[property];
                lighting[property] = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);
                task.wait(0.2);
                lighting[property] = initialValue;
            end)
        end;

        flashPropertyToWhite('Ambient');
        flashPropertyToWhite('ColorShift_Bottom');
        flashPropertyToWhite('ColorShift_Top');
        task.delay(math.random(), function()
            --play random sound inside Thundersounds
            local sound = THUNDER_SOUNDS[math.random(1, #THUNDER_SOUNDS)];
            sound:Play();
        end);
    end);

    Rain:SetLightEmission(0);
end;

function WeatherController:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    RandomDecimal = self.Shared.NumberUtil.RandomDecimal;
    Rain = self.Modules.Rain;
    AmbientSoundController = self.Controllers.Environment.AmbientSoundController;
end;



return WeatherController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/FireHoseReplicationController.lua ---

--[[
    FireHoseReplicationController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Fire Hose Replication Controller
-- Khizzer
-- March 21, 2023

local PhysicsService = game:GetService('PhysicsService');

local Trove;
local NetworkController;
local FireHoseReplicationController = {}

local SMOOTH_PLASTIC = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local HOSE_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(193, 190, 66);
local HOSE_DIAMETER = 0.447;
local HOSE_SEGMENT_DISTANCE = 0.5;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local function CreateBase(char: Model, folder: Folder, count: number, attackLine: Tool): nil
	local newPart = Instance.new('Part')
	newPart.Color = HOSE_COLOR
	newPart.Material = SMOOTH_PLASTIC
	newPart.Shape = 'Ball'
	newPart.Locked = true
	newPart.CanCollide = false
	newPart.Anchored = true
	newPart.Name = count

	local lineEnd = attackLine.LineEnd;
	local hosePos = lineEnd.Position
	local targetPos = Vector3.new(0, -100, 0)

	local Params = RaycastParams.new()
	Params.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Blacklist
	Params.FilterDescendantsInstances = {char}
	Params.CollisionGroup = 'Default'
	local RaycastResult = workspace:Raycast(hosePos, targetPos, Params)

	local NewYPosition = RaycastResult.Position.Y + (HOSE_DIAMETER / 2)

	newPart.Size = Vector3.new(HOSE_DIAMETER, HOSE_DIAMETER, HOSE_DIAMETER)
	newPart.Position = Vector3.new(RaycastResult.Position.X, NewYPosition, RaycastResult.Position.Z)

	newPart.Parent = folder

    newPart.CollisionGroup = 'FireHose'

	return newPart
end;

local function CreateConnection(connection1: Part, connection2: Part, folder: Folder, canDelete: boolean, attackLine: Tool): nil
	local newPart = Instance.new('Part');
	newPart.Color = HOSE_COLOR;
	newPart.Material = SMOOTH_PLASTIC;
	newPart.Shape = Enum.PartType.Cylinder;
	newPart.Locked = true;
	newPart.CanCollide = false;
	newPart.Anchored = true;

	if canDelete then
		if not connection1:FindFirstChild('NextPart') then
			local nextValue = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
			nextValue.Name = 'NextPart';
			nextValue.Value = newPart;
			nextValue.Parent = connection1;
		else
			connection1.NextPart.Value = newPart;
		end;
	end;

	local n  = HOSE_DIAMETER

    --Get all the x,y,z positions of connection 1 and 2
	local x1 = connection1.Position.X
	local x2 = connection2.Position.X
	local y1 = connection1.Position.Y
	local y2 = connection2.Position.Y
	local z1 = connection1.Position.Z
	local z2 = connection2.Position.Z

	--Assuming Positive
	local L =  math.sqrt((x1-x2)^2+(z1-z2)^2)
	local length = math.sqrt(L^2 + (y2-y1)^2)

	if x2 - x1 < 0 and z2 - z1 > 0 then
        L *= -1;
	end

	if x2 - x1 < 0 and z2 - z1 < 0 then
        L *= -1
	end

	local angle  = -(math.deg(math.atan((z1-z2)/(x1-x2))))
	local angleV = -(math.deg(math.atan((y1-y2)/L)))
	local posX   = (x1+x2)/2
	local posY   = (y1+y2)/2
	local posZ   = (z1+z2)/2

	if x2 - x1 == 0 then
		angleV = -angleV
	end

	if x2 - x1 < 0 and z2 - z1 == 0 then
		angleV = -angleV
	end

	if x2 - x1 == 0 and z2 - z1 == 0 then
		angle = 90
	end

	newPart.Size = Vector3.new(length, n, n)
	newPart.Orientation = Vector3.new(0, angle, angleV)
	newPart.Position = Vector3.new(posX, posY, posZ)

    newPart.CollisionGroup = 'FireHose';

	newPart.Parent = folder

	return newPart
end

local function CreateFinalPart(connection1: Part, connection2: Part, parent: Instance): nil

	local newPart = Instance.new('Part')
	newPart.Color = HOSE_COLOR
	newPart.Material = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic
	newPart.Shape = 'Cylinder'
	newPart.Locked = true
	newPart.CanCollide = false
	newPart.Anchored = true

	local n  = HOSE_DIAMETER;
	local x1 = connection1.Position.X
	local x2 = connection2.Position.X
	local y1 = connection1.Position.Y
	local y2 = connection2.Position.Y
	local z1 = connection1.Position.Z
	local z2 = connection2.Position.Z

	--Assuming Positive
	local L =  math.sqrt((x1-x2)^2+(z1-z2)^2)
	local Length = math.sqrt(L^2 + (y2-y1)^2)

	if x2 - x1 < 0 and z2 - z1 > 0 then
		L = -L
	end

	if x2 - x1 < 0 and z2 - z1 < 0 then
		L = -L
	end

	local Angle  = -(math.deg(math.atan((z1-z2)/(x1-x2))))
	local AngleV = -(math.deg(math.atan((y1-y2)/L)))
	local PosX   = (x1+x2)/2
	local PosY   = (y1+y2)/2
	local PosZ   = (z1+z2)/2

	if x2 - x1 == 0 then
		AngleV = -AngleV
	end

	if x2 - x1 < 0 and z2 - z1 == 0 then
		AngleV = -AngleV
	end

	if x2 - x1 == 0 and z2 - z1 == 0 then
		Angle = 90
	end

	newPart.Size = Vector3.new(Length, n, n)
	newPart.Orientation = Vector3.new(0, Angle, AngleV)
	newPart.Position = Vector3.new(PosX, PosY, PosZ)

	newPart.Parent = parent

	return newPart

end

function FireHoseReplicationController:Start()
    local HoseStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
    HoseStorage.Name = 'HoseStorage';
    HoseStorage.Parent = workspace;

	NetworkController.Connect('FireHoseReplication', function(vfrsPlayer, truckPart)
        local character = vfrsPlayer.Character;
        local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild('Humanoid');

        if not humanoid then return; end;
        local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool');
        if not tool then return; end;

        local isAttackLine = (tool.Name == 'Attack Line');
        if not isAttackLine then return; end;

        local lineEnd = tool:FindFirstChild('LineEnd');

        local trove = Trove.new();
        trove:AttachToInstance(tool);

        local plrFolder = Instance.new('Folder');
        plrFolder.Name = vfrsPlayer.Name;
        plrFolder.Parent = HoseStorage;

        local nodeStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
        nodeStorage.Name = 'NodeStorage';
        nodeStorage.Parent = plrFolder;

        local connectionStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
        connectionStorage.Name = 'ConnectionStorage';
        connectionStorage.Parent = plrFolder;

        trove:Add(plrFolder);
        trove:Add(nodeStorage);
        trove:Add(connectionStorage);

        local function GetDistanceToGround(attackLine)
            local lineEnd = attackLine.LineEnd;
            local hosePos = lineEnd.Position
            local targetPos = Vector3.new(0, -100, 0)
            local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new()
            raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Blacklist
            raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {character}
            raycastParams.CollisionGroup = 'Default'
            local raycastResult = workspace:Raycast(hosePos, targetPos, raycastParams)

            return raycastResult.Position + Vector3.new(0, (HOSE_DIAMETER / 2), 0)
        end;

        local count = 0;
        local startNode = CreateBase(character, nodeStorage, count, tool);
        count += 1;

        local startConnection = CreateConnection(startNode, truckPart, connectionStorage, false, tool);
        startConnection.Name = 'First';
        count += 1;

        local lastCharacterPos: Vector3?;

        local lastNode;

        local finalConnectingPart = {};

        trove:BindToRenderStep('FireHoseReplicationController'..vfrsPlayer.Name, Enum.RenderPriority.Last.Value, function()
            local characterPos = character.PrimaryPart.Position;
            if lastCharacterPos then
                if (lastCharacterPos - characterPos).Magnitude == 0 then return; end;
            end;

            lastCharacterPos = characterPos;
            local nearestNode = nodeStorage:FindFirstChildOfClass('Part');
            for _,v in next, nodeStorage:GetChildren() do
                if (v.Position - GetDistanceToGround(tool)).Magnitude < (nearestNode.Position - GetDistanceToGround(tool)).Magnitude then
                    nearestNode = v;
                end
            end

            if nearestNode then
                if tonumber(nearestNode.Name) < count then
                    for _, v in next, nodeStorage:GetChildren() do
                        if tonumber(v.Name) > tonumber(nearestNode.Name) then
                            if v:FindFirstChild('NextPart') and v.NextPart.Value then
                                v.NextPart.Value:Destroy();
                            end;
                            v:Destroy();
                        end;
                    end;

                    if nearestNode:FindFirstChild('NextPart') and nearestNode.NextPart.Value then
                        nearestNode.NextPart.Value:Destroy();
                    end;
                end

                if (nearestNode.Position - GetDistanceToGround(tool)).Magnitude >= HOSE_SEGMENT_DISTANCE then
                    local newNode = CreateBase(character, nodeStorage, count, tool);
                    count += 1;
                    CreateConnection(nearestNode, newNode, connectionStorage, true, tool);
                end;
                lastNode = nearestNode;
            end

            for _,v in next, finalConnectingPart do
                v:Destroy();
            end;
            table.insert(finalConnectingPart, CreateFinalPart(lastNode, lineEnd, plrFolder))
        end)

        trove:Add(tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
            if vfrsPlayer == localPlayer then
                NetworkController.Send('DETACH_ATTACK_LINE', tool); --tell server to delete watercapacity objval
            end;

            for _,v in next, finalConnectingPart do
                v:Destroy();
            end

            task.wait(.5);
            trove:Clean();
        end))
    end)
end


function FireHoseReplicationController:Init()
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end


return FireHoseReplicationController

local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");
local Packages = ReplicatedStorage.Packages

local InstanceCache = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.InstanceCache);

local UP_VELOCITY = Vector3.new(0, 7, 0);

local wait;
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local mathRandom = math.random;

local Debris;
local Raycast;

local IMPACT_SOUNDS = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('ImpactSounds', 10);
local BulletHolePart = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('BulletHole', 10);

local bulletCache = InstanceCache.new(BulletHolePart, 300);

local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local bulletCasingPrefab = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild('Storage'):WaitForChild('Gun'):WaitForChild('BulletCasing');

local GunReplicationController = {};

function GunReplicationController:Start()
    math.randomseed(tick());

	self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('GunEffect', function(gun)
        if not gun then return; end;
        if not gun:FindFirstChild('Barrel') then return; end;

        local barrel = gun.Barrel;
        --if (camera.CFrame.Position - barrel.Position).Magnitude > 200 then return; end;

        local flash = barrel.Flash;
        local light = barrel.Light;
        local smoke = barrel.Smoke;

        local bulletCasing;
        if gun.Name ~= 'Pepper Gun' then
            local bulletCasingEjectorCFrame = gun.BulletCasingEjector.CFrame;
            bulletCasing = bulletCasingPrefab:Clone();
            bulletCasing.CFrame = bulletCasingEjectorCFrame;
            bulletCasing.Velocity = (-bulletCasingEjectorCFrame.RightVector * mathRandom(6, 8)) + (-bulletCasingEjectorCFrame.UpVector * mathRandom(1.2, 1.5)) + UP_VELOCITY;
            bulletCasing.RotVelocity = newVector3(mathRandom(8), mathRandom(8), mathRandom(8));
            bulletCasing.Parent = workspace;
        end

        barrel.Shoot:Play();
        flash.Enabled = true;
        if gun.Name ~= 'Pepper Gun' then light.Enabled = true; end;
        smoke.Enabled = true;
        wait(0.2);
        if bulletCasing then bulletCasing:Destroy(); end;
        flash.Enabled = false;
        light.Enabled = false;
        smoke.Enabled = false;
    end);

    self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('TaserEffect', function(taser, torso)
        coroutineWrap(function()
            local active = true;
            local TorsoPart = Instance.new('Part');
            TorsoPart.Name = 'TorsoPart'
            TorsoPart.Parent = workspace.BulletStorage;
            TorsoPart.Anchored = true;
            TorsoPart.Transparency = 1;
            TorsoPart.CanCollide = false;
            TorsoPart.Size = torso.Size;

            local TaserPart = Instance.new('Part');
            TaserPart.Name = 'TaserPart';
            TaserPart.Parent = workspace.BulletStorage;
            TaserPart.Anchored = true;
            TaserPart.Transparency = 1;
            TaserPart.CanCollide = false;
            TaserPart.Size = taser.Barrel.Size;

            local TorsoAttachment1 = Instance.new('Attachment');
            local TorsoAttachment2 = Instance.new('Attachment');
            local TaserAttachment = Instance.new('Attachment');

            TorsoAttachment1.Parent = TorsoPart;
            TorsoAttachment1.Position = Vector3.new(0, 0.118, 0)
            TorsoAttachment2.Parent = TorsoPart;
            TorsoAttachment2.Position = Vector3.new(0, -0.019, 0)
            TaserAttachment.Parent = TaserPart;

            local coil1 = Instance.new('SpringConstraint');
            local coil2 = Instance.new('SpringConstraint')

            coil1.Parent = TaserPart;
            coil1.Color = BrickColor.new('Fossil');
            coil1.Coils = 4;
            coil1.Radius = 0.1
            coil1.Thickness = 0.01;
            coil1.Visible = true;
            coil1.Attachment0 = TaserAttachment;
            coil1.Attachment1 = TorsoAttachment1;
            
            coil2.Parent = TaserPart;
            coil2.Color = BrickColor.new('Fossil');
            coil2.Coils = 3;
            coil2.Radius = 0.1
            coil2.Thickness = 0.01;
            coil2.Visible = true;
            coil2.Attachment0 = TaserAttachment;
            coil2.Attachment1 = TorsoAttachment2;

            local taserRemovedConnection = taser.Parent.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child)
                if child.Name == 'X-26' then
                    active = false;
                end;
            end)

            coroutineWrap(function()
                while true do
                    if not active or not taser then
                        TorsoPart:Destroy();
                        TaserPart:Destroy();
                        taserRemovedConnection:Disconnect();
                        taserRemovedConnection = nil;
                        break;
                    end;
                    if taser then
                        TorsoPart.CFrame = torso.CFrame;
                        TaserPart.CFrame = taser.Barrel.CFrame;
                    end;
                    task.wait()
                end;
            end)();
            task.wait(4)
            active = false;
        end)();
    end)

    self.Controllers.NetworkController.Connect('CreateBulletHoles', function(pos, barrelPos, direction, plr)
        local hit, _position, normal, _material = Raycast.FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(barrelPos, direction, {plr.Character});
            if not hit then return; end;
            if not hit:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;
            local bulletHolePart = bulletCache:GetInstance();
            local position = CFrame.lookAt(pos, pos - normal) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(180), 0, 0)
            bulletHolePart.CFrame = position;
            bulletHolePart.Decal.Color3 = hit.Color;
            bulletHolePart.Massless = true;
            local color = ColorSequence.new({
                ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)),
                ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.145, hit.Color),
                ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, hit.Color)
            });

            local isCar = hit:FindFirstAncestor('Cars');
            local isWheel = hit.Name == 'Wheel';

            if isCar or hit.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid') then
                local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
                weld.Part0 = hit;
                weld.Part1 = bulletHolePart;
                weld.Parent = bulletHolePart;
                bulletHolePart.Anchored = false;
            end;
            bulletHolePart.Spark.Enabled = true;
            bulletHolePart.Spark.Color = color;
            local sound = if isCar and not isWheel then IMPACT_SOUNDS['Metal'] elseif IMPACT_SOUNDS:FindFirstChild(hit.Material.Name) then IMPACT_SOUNDS[hit.Material.Name] else IMPACT_SOUNDS.Default;
            sound = sound:Clone();
            sound.Parent = bulletHolePart;
            bulletHolePart.Parent = workspace.BulletStorage;
            sound:Play();
            task.delay(0.3, function() bulletHolePart.Spark.Enabled = false; end)
            task.delay(10, function()
                if bulletHolePart:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
                    bulletHolePart.WeldConstraint:Destroy();
                end;
                bulletCache:ReturnInstance(bulletHolePart);
            end);
            --Debris:AddItem(bulletHolePart.Spark, 0.3);
            --Debris:AddItem(bulletHolePart, 10);
    end)
end;

function GunReplicationController:Init()
	wait = self.Shared.Wait;
    Debris = self.Shared.DebrisGobbler;
    Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast;
end;

return GunReplicationController;

local HelicopterController = {}

        if event == 'Enter' then
            currentHelicopter = Helicopter.new(helicopter);
        elseif event == 'Exit' then
            currentHelicopter:Destroy();
            currentHelicopter = nil;
        end;
    end)
end;

    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Helicopter/HelicopterController_contents/Helicopter.lua ---

--[[
    Helicopter (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Helicopter → HelicopterController
    Parent: HelicopterController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Helicopter
-- Khizzer
-- April 2, 2023



local ContextActionService = game:GetService('ContextActionService');
local UserInputService = game:GetService('UserInputService');

local PID;
local Trove;

local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');

local Helicopter = {}
Helicopter.__index = Helicopter;

function Helicopter.new(helicopter)
	local self = setmetatable({}, Helicopter);

	self.Helicopter = helicopter;
	self.Airframe = self.Helicopter.Airframe;
	self.Platform = self.Airframe.Platform;
	self.Skid = self.Airframe.Skid;
	self.Seat = self.Airframe.VehicleSeat;

	self.EngineRunning = false;

	self.Rotor = self.Airframe.MainRotor;
	self.TailRotor = self.Airframe.TailRotor;

	self.RotorHinge = self.Platform.RotorHingeConstraint;
	self.TailHinge = self.Platform.TailHingeConstraint;

	self.RotorVectorForce = self.Platform.RotorVectorForce;
	self.TailRotorVectorForce = self.Platform.TailRotorVectorForce;

	self.Torque = self.Platform.Torque;

	self.Pitch = 0;
	self.Roll = 0;
	self.ForwardTorque = 0;
	self.SideTorque = 0;
	self.TailForce = 0;
	self.HoverForce = 0;

	self.PitchPID = PID.new(-70, 70, 0.4, 0, 10);
	self.RollPID = PID.new(-60, 60, 1, 0, 5);
	self.ForwardTorquePID = PID.new(-8, 8, 0.5, 0, 20);
	self.SideTorquePID = PID.new(-2, 2, 0.2, 0, 10);
	self.TailPID = PID.new(-8, 8, 190, 0, 1);
	self.HoverPID = PID.new(130, 300, 5, 1, 1);

    local debugFolder = Instance.new('Folder', workspace);
    debugFolder.Name = '!HELICOPTER_DEBUG';

	self.PitchPID:Debug('Pitch', debugFolder);
	self.RollPID:Debug('Roll', debugFolder);
	self.ForwardTorquePID:Debug('ForwardTorque', debugFolder);
	self.SideTorquePID:Debug('SideTorque', debugFolder);
	self.TailPID:Debug('Tail', debugFolder);
	self.HoverPID:Debug('Hover', debugFolder);

	self.MaxSpeed = 80;
	self.MaxRotationSpeed = 80;

    self.Trove = Trove.new();

	self:ConnectKeybinds();
	self:ConnectEvents();
	return self;
end

function Helicopter:ConnectKeybinds()
	ContextActionService:BindAction('EngineToggle', function(action, inputState)
		if inputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then return; end;

		self.EngineRunning = not self.EngineRunning;

		local angularVelocity = 0;

		if RunService:IsStudio() then
			self.RotorHinge.MotorMaxAcceleration = 10;
			self.TailHinge.MotorMaxAcceleration = 10;
		end;

		angularVelocity = (self.EngineRunning and self.MaxRotationSpeed) or 0;

		self.RotorHinge.AngularVelocity = angularVelocity;
		self.TailHinge.AngularVelocity = -angularVelocity;
	end, false, Enum.KeyCode.Y)

	ContextActionService:BindAction('Flip', function(action, inputState)
		if inputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then return; end;

		if self.FlipDebounce then return; end;
		local bodyPosition = Instance.new('BodyPosition');
		bodyPosition.MaxForce = Vector3.new(99999, 99999, 99999);
		bodyPosition.Position = self.Seat.Position + Vector3.new(0, 3.5, 0);
		bodyPosition.P = 12000;
		local bodyGyro = Instance.new('BodyGyro');
		bodyPosition.Parent = self.Seat;
		bodyGyro.Parent = self.Seat;
		task.wait(3);
		bodyPosition:Destroy();
		bodyGyro:Destroy();
		task.wait(0.5);
		self.FlipDebounce = false;
	end, false, Enum.KeyCode.F)
end

function Helicopter:GetRudder()
	local isADown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A);
	local isDDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D);
	local isZDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Z);
	local isCDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.C);

	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift) then
		if isZDown == isCDown then return 0; end;

		if isZDown then return 1; end;
		if isCDown then return -1; end;
	else
		if isADown == isDDown then return 0; end;

		if isADown then return 1; end;

		if isDDown then return -1; end;
	end;
end

function Helicopter:GetCollective()
	local isQDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Q);
	local isEDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.E);


	if (isQDown == isEDown) then return 0; end;

	if isQDown then return -1; end;
	if isEDown then return 1; end;

end;

function Helicopter:GetCyclic()
	local isWDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W);
	local isADown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A);
	local isSDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S);
	local isDDown = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D);

	if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift) then
		local x;
		local y;

		if isADown == isDDown then
			x = 0;
		else
			x = (isADown and -1) or 1
		end;

		if isWDown == isSDown then
			y = 0;
		else
			y = (isSDown and -1) or 1;
		end;

		return Vector2.new(x, y);
	else
		local x = 0
		local y;

		if isWDown == isSDown then
			y = 0;
		else
			y = (isSDown and -1) or 1;
		end;
		return Vector2.new(x, y);
	end
end

function Helicopter:IsLanding()
	local skid = self.Skid;

	local moving = false;
	if skid.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude < 0.01 then
		moving = skid.AssemblyAngularVelocity.Magnitude < 0.01;
	end;

	if not moving then
		return false;
	end;

	for _,v in next, skid:GetTouchingParts() do
		if not v:IsDescendantOf(self.Helicopter) and v.Anchored then
			return true;
		end
	end;

	return false;
end;

function Helicopter:CalculatePIDs()
	local platform = self.Platform;

	local mass = platform.AssemblyMass;
	local orientation = platform.Orientation;

	local orientationX = orientation.X;
	local oreintationZ = orientation.Z;

	local velocity = platform.AssemblyLinearVelocity;

	local relativeDirection = platform.CFrame:VectorToObjectSpace(velocity);
	local airSpeed = Vector3.new(relativeDirection.X, 0, relativeDirection.Z);

	local forwardsSpeed = 0;
	local sidewaysSpeed = 0;

	if relativeDirection.Magnitude > 0.01 then
		forwardsSpeed = velocity.Unit:Dot(platform.CFrame.LookVector);
		sidewaysSpeed = velocity.Unit:Cross(Vector3.yAxis):Dot(platform.CFrame.LookVector);
	else
		forwardsSpeed = 0;
		sidewaysSpeed = 0;
	end;

	local landing = false;

	if forwardsSpeed == 0 then
		landing = false
		if sidewaysSpeed == 0 then
			landing = self:IsLanding();
		end;
	end;

	local rudderAngle = (landing and 0) or (self:GetRudder());

	local cyclicVector = self:GetCyclic();
	local pitchAngle = (landing and 0 ) or cyclicVector.Y * 90;

	local rollAngle = (landing and 0) or cyclicVector.X * 30

	self.TailForce = self.TailPID:Calculate(rudderAngle, platform.CFrame:VectorToObjectSpace(platform.AssemblyAngularVelocity).Y) * mass;
	self.Pitch = -self.PitchPID:Calculate(pitchAngle, airSpeed.Magnitude * forwardsSpeed);
	self.Roll = self.RollPID:Calculate(-rollAngle, airSpeed.Magnitude * sidewaysSpeed);
	self.ForwardTorque = -self.ForwardTorquePID:Calculate(self.Pitch, orientationX);
	self.SideTorque = self.SideTorquePID:Calculate(self.Roll, oreintationZ);

	local collective = self:GetCollective();
	if landing and collective == 0 then
		collective = -1;
	end;

	self.HoverForce = self.HoverPID:Calculate(collective * 20, velocity.Y) * mass;
end

function Helicopter:ConnectEvents()
	self.Trove:Add(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dT)
		local platform = self.Platform;

		self:CalculatePIDs();
		local mass = platform.AssemblyMass;
		local forwardForce = (self.ForwardTorque * self.MaxSpeed) * mass;
		local sideForce = (self.SideTorque * self.MaxSpeed) * mass;

		local rotorForce = math.abs(platform.CFrame:VectorToObjectSpace(self.Rotor.AssemblyAngularVelocity).Y) / self.MaxRotationSpeed;

		self.RotorVectorForce.Force = Vector3.new(rotorForce * self.HoverForce, 0, 0);
		self.TailRotorVectorForce.Force = Vector3.new(self.TailForce * rotorForce, 0, 0);
		self.Torque.Torque = Vector3.new(0, forwardForce * rotorForce, sideForce * rotorForce);
	end))
end

function Helicopter:Destroy()
    self.Trove:Destroy();
end;

function Helicopter:Init()
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
    PID = self.Shared.PID;
end;

return Helicopter;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Helicopter/HelicopterReplicationController.lua ---

--[[
    HelicopterReplicationController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Helicopter
    Parent: Helicopter
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Helicopter Replication Controller
-- Khizzer
-- April 2, 2023

local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');

local UPDATE_COOLDOWN = 0.1;

local timeSinceLastUpdate = 0;

local HelicopterReplicationController = {}

function HelicopterReplicationController:Start()
    local helicopters = workspace:WaitForChild('Helicopters');

    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dT)
        timeSinceLastUpdate += dT;

        if timeSinceLastUpdate < UPDATE_COOLDOWN then return; end;
        timeSinceLastUpdate = 0;

        for _,v in next, helicopters:GetChildren() do
            local airframe = v:FindFirstChild('Airframe');
            if not airframe then continue; end;

            local platform: Part? = airframe:FindFirstChild('Platform');
            if not platform then continue; end;

            local mainRotor = airframe:FindFirstChild('MainRotor');
            if not mainRotor then continue; end;

            local mainRotorAttachment = mainRotor:FindFirstChild('Attachment');
            if not mainRotorAttachment then continue; end;

            local mainRotorSound = mainRotorAttachment:FindFirstChild('Sound');
            if not mainRotorSound then continue; end;

            local rotorSpeed = mainRotor.AssemblyAngularVelocity;

            --The speed as a fraction of max speed
            local speed = math.abs(platform.CFrame:VectorToObjectSpace(rotorSpeed).Y) / 80;
            
            mainRotorSound.Volume = speed;
            mainRotorSound.PlaybackSpeed = 0.5 + (0.8 * speed);
            mainRotorSound:Play();
        end;
    end)
end;


return HelicopterReplicationController

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/InteractionController.lua ---

--[[
    InteractionController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Interaction;

type Interaction = {
	Part: BasePart | Attachment;
	Priority: number;
	IsInWorkspace: boolean;
	EvaluateCondition: () -> boolean;
	Show: () -> nil;
	Hide: () -> nil;
	Destroy: () -> nil;
}

type InteractionModule = {
	Get: (part: BasePart | Attachment) -> (string?, Enum.KeyCode?, number?, number?);
	Event: (part: BasePart | Attachment) -> nil;
};

local char;
local rootPart;

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local ProximityPromptService = game:GetService('ProximityPromptService');
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');

local tagToInteractionModules: {[string]: { {InteractionModule} }} = {};
local interactionsToProximityPrompts: {[Interaction]: ProximityPrompt} = {};

local visibleProximityPrompts: {ProximityPrompt} = {};

local availableInteractions = {};

local oldInteractions = {};
local visibleInteractions = {};

local CopyShallow;

local function AddTagToInteractionMap(tag: string, interaction: InteractionModule)
	if not tagToInteractionModules[tag] then
		tagToInteractionModules[tag] = {};
	end;

	table.insert(tagToInteractionModules[tag], interaction);
end;

local function GetAttachmentWorldCFrame(attachment: Attachment): CFrame
	return attachment.Parent.CFrame:toWorldSpace(attachment.CFrame)
end;

local function GetAttachmentWorldPosition(attachment: Attachment): Vector3
	return GetAttachmentWorldCFrame(attachment).Position
end;

local function SetInteraction(tag: string, interactionModules: {InteractionModule})
	for _, instance in CollectionService:GetTagged(tag) do
		local proximityPrompt = Instance.new('ProximityPrompt');
		proximityPrompt.KeyboardKeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.F7;
		proximityPrompt.MaxActivationDistance = 7 -- modify this
		proximityPrompt.Style = Enum.ProximityPromptStyle.Custom;
		proximityPrompt.Exclusivity = Enum.ProximityPromptExclusivity.AlwaysShow;
		proximityPrompt.RequiresLineOfSight = false;
		proximityPrompt.ClickablePrompt = false;
		proximityPrompt.Parent = instance;

		for _, interaction in interactionModules do
			interactionsToProximityPrompts[Interaction.new(instance, interaction, proximityPrompt)] = proximityPrompt;
		end;
	end;

	CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal(tag):Connect(function(instance)
		local proximityPrompt = Instance.new('ProximityPrompt');
		proximityPrompt.KeyboardKeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.F7;
		proximityPrompt.MaxActivationDistance = 7 -- modify this
		proximityPrompt.Style = Enum.ProximityPromptStyle.Custom;
		proximityPrompt.Exclusivity = Enum.ProximityPromptExclusivity.AlwaysShow;
		proximityPrompt.RequiresLineOfSight = false;
		proximityPrompt.ClickablePrompt = false;
		proximityPrompt.Parent = instance;

		for _, interaction in interactionModules do
			interactionsToProximityPrompts[Interaction.new(instance, interaction, proximityPrompt)] = proximityPrompt;
		end
	end);

	CollectionService:GetInstanceRemovedSignal(tag):Connect(function(instance)
		for interaction, proximityPrompt in interactionsToProximityPrompts do
			if interaction.Part == instance then
                interaction:Destroy();
				interactionsToProximityPrompts[interaction] = nil;
			end;
		end;
	end);
end;

local InteractionController = {};

function InteractionController:CharacterAdded(_char)
	if not _char then return; end;
	char = _char;
	rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

function InteractionController:_evaluatePrompts()
	visibleInteractions = {};

	for _, v in visibleProximityPrompts do
		for interaction, proximityPrompt in interactionsToProximityPrompts do
			if proximityPrompt == v then
				if interaction:EvaluateCondition() then
					table.insert(visibleInteractions, interaction);
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;

	table.sort(visibleInteractions, function(a, b)
		if a.Priority == b.Priority then
			if a.Part:IsA('Attachment') then
				return (GetAttachmentWorldPosition(a.Part) - rootPart.Position).Magnitude < (GetAttachmentWorldPosition(b.Part) - rootPart.Position).Magnitude;
			end;
			return (a.Part.Position - rootPart.Position).Magnitude < (b.Part.Position - rootPart.Position).Magnitude;
		end;
		return a.Priority > b.Priority;
	end);
end;


function InteractionController:Start()
	ProximityPromptService.MaxPromptsVisible = 50;

	repeat task.wait() until rootPart;

    for i, v in script.Parent:WaitForChild('Interactions'):GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Folder') then
            local folderName = v.Name;
            for i2, v2 in v:GetChildren() do
                AddTagToInteractionMap(folderName, require(v2));
            end;
        else
            AddTagToInteractionMap(v.Name, require(v));
        end;
		table.freeze(tagToInteractionModules[v.Name]);
    end;

	table.freeze(tagToInteractionModules);

	for tag, interactionModules in tagToInteractionModules do
		SetInteraction(tag, interactionModules);
	end;

	ProximityPromptService.PromptShown:Connect(function(prompt, inputType)
		table.insert(visibleProximityPrompts, prompt);
	end)

	ProximityPromptService.PromptHidden:Connect(function(prompt, inputType)
		local index = table.find(visibleProximityPrompts, prompt);
		if index then
			table.remove(visibleProximityPrompts, index);
		end;
	end)

	RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
		if not rootPart then return; end;
		availableInteractions = {};
		local shortestDistance = 7;
		local currentPriority = 1;

		self:_evaluatePrompts();

		--print(`{#visibleInteractions} visible interactions`);
		if #visibleInteractions > 0 then
			--availableInteractions = CopyShallow(availableInteractions);
		else
			availableInteractions = {};
		end;

		for _,v in visibleInteractions do
			local part = v.Part;
			local partPos = (part:IsA('Attachment') and GetAttachmentWorldPosition(part)) or (part.Position);
			local availableInteraction = availableInteractions[1];
			if v.IsInWorkspace == true then
				if availableInteraction and part == availableInteraction.Part then
					table.insert(availableInteractions, v);
				else
					local distance = (partPos - rootPart.Position).Magnitude;
					if v.Priority >= currentPriority then
						if distance < shortestDistance then
							availableInteractions = {v};
							shortestDistance = distance;
							currentPriority = v.Priority;
						end;
					end;
				end
			end
		end

		for _,v in oldInteractions do
			if not table.find(availableInteractions, v) then
				v:Hide();
			end
		end

		for _,v in availableInteractions do
			v:Show();
		end;

		oldInteractions = CopyShallow(availableInteractions);
	end)
end;

function InteractionController:Init()
    Interaction = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Interaction')));
	CopyShallow = self.Shared.TableUtil.CopyShallow;
end;

return InteractionController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/InteractionController_contents/Interaction.lua ---

--[[
    Interaction (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → InteractionController
    Parent: InteractionController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Interaction = {};
Interaction.__index = Interaction;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local playerGUI = localPlayer:WaitForChild('PlayerGui');

local ContextActionUtility = require(script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Modules.ContextActionUtility);

local inputService = game:GetService('UserInputService');
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local ContextActionService = game:GetService('ContextActionService');
local inputBegan = inputService.InputBegan;
local inputEnded = inputService.InputEnded;

local Map;

local mathClamp = math.clamp;

Map = function(n, start, stop, newStart, newStop)
    local value = ((n - start) / (stop - start)) * (newStop - newStart) + newStart;

    if newStart < newStop then
        return mathClamp(value, newStart, newStop);
    else
        return mathClamp(value, newStop, newStart);
    end;
end;



local interactionStorage = localPlayer.PlayerScripts:WaitForChild('Storage'):WaitForChild('Interaction');
local interactGUI = interactionStorage.InteractGUI;
local show = interactionStorage.Show;

local KEY_BTN_PRESSED_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 29);
local KEY_BTN_DEFAULT_SIZE = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 32);
local DISABLED_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(187, 75, 75)
local DISABLED_COLOR_2 = Color3.fromRGB(194, 35, 35)

local newUDim2 = UDim2.new;
local getChildren = workspace.GetChildren;

local function AddNameLabel(part, name, key, event)
	local nameLabel = interactGUI.NameLabel:Clone();
	local keyBtn = nameLabel.KeyBtn;
	keyBtn.KeyLabel.Text = key.Name;
	nameLabel.Name = name;
	nameLabel.Text = name;
	nameLabel.Visible = true;
--[[ 	keyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		event(part);
	end); ]]

	if #getChildren(interactGUI) == 2 then
		interactGUI.Adornee = part;
		interactGUI.Enabled = true;
	end;

	nameLabel.Parent = interactGUI;

	nameLabel.Size = newUDim2(0, nameLabel.TextBounds.X + 12, 0, 32);

	if string.find(name, 'DISABLED') then
		keyBtn.ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR;
		nameLabel.BackgroundImage.ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR_2
	end

	return nameLabel;
end;

function Interaction.new(part, interaction, proximityPrompt)
	local self = setmetatable({}, Interaction);

	self.NameLabel = nil;
	self.Interaction = interaction;
	self.Part = (part:IsA('Model') and part.PrimaryPart) or  part;
	self.InputBegan = nil;
	self.InputEnded = nil;
	self.IsInWorkspace = false;
	self.IsVisible = false;
	self.Priority = 1;
	self.DefaultPriority = 1;
	self.ProximityPrompt = proximityPrompt;

	self.UniqueIdentifier = HttpService:GenerateGUID(false);

	if interaction.Priority ~= nil then
		self.Priority = interaction.Priority
		self.DefaultPriority = interaction.Priority
	else
		self.Priority = 1
	end

	self.IsInWorkspace = part:IsDescendantOf(workspace);
	self.AncestryChangedConnection = part.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
		self.IsInWorkspace = part:IsDescendantOf(workspace);
	end);

	return self;
end;

function Interaction:Destroy()
	self.AncestryChangedConnection:Disconnect();
	self.AncestryChangedConnection = nil;
	self.ProximityPrompt:Destroy();
end;

function Interaction:SetText(text: string)
	if self.NameLabel then
		self.NameLabel.Text = text;
		self.NameLabel.Size = newUDim2(0, self.NameLabel.TextBounds.X + 12, 0, 32);
	end;
end;

function Interaction:EvaluateCondition()
	local interaction = self.Interaction;
	local part = self.Part;
	local name: string?, key: Enum.KeyCode?, interactionTime: number?, priority: number?  = interaction.Get(part);

	self.Priority = if priority then priority else self.DefaultPriority;

	if name ~= nil then --if interaction is gonna get showed, keep the name updated
		local lastName = self.LastName or ''
		if lastName ~= name then
			if self.NameLabel then
				self:SetText(name);
			end;
		end;
	end;

	self.LastName = name;
	if not name then return false else return true; end;
end;

function Interaction:Show()
	local interactGUIEnabled = interactGUI.Enabled;
	local enabled = self.NameLabel;

	local interaction = self.Interaction;
	local part = self.Part;
	local name: string?, key: Enum.KeyCode?, interactionTime: number?, priority: number?  = interaction.Get(part);

	if enabled and (not name) then
		self:Hide();
		self.IsVisible = false
		return;
	else
		self.IsVisible = true
	end;
	if enabled then return; end;
	if not name then return; end;
	if part:GetAttribute('InteractionLabel') then
		name = part:GetAttribute('InteractionLabel')
	end

	local event = interaction.Event;

	local nameLabel = AddNameLabel(part, name, key, event);
	self.NameLabel = nameLabel;

	local keyBtn = nameLabel.KeyBtn;
	local progressBar: ImageLabel = nameLabel.BackgroundImage.Progress;

	local uniqueIdentifier = self.UniqueIdentifier;

	local interactionInterrupted = false;

	local timedInteractionDown = false;

	self.InputEnded = inputEnded:Connect(function(input, onGUI)
		if onGUI then return; end;

		if input.KeyCode == key then
			keyBtn.Size = KEY_BTN_DEFAULT_SIZE;
			if timedInteractionDown then
				interactionInterrupted = true;
				timedInteractionDown = false;
			end
			progressBar.Visible = false;
			progressBar.Size = newUDim2(0, 0, 1, 0);
		end;
	end);

	local deltaT;

	ContextActionUtility:BindAction(uniqueIdentifier, function(actionName, inputState, inputObject)
		if inputState == Enum.UserInputState.Begin then
			keyBtn.Size = KEY_BTN_PRESSED_SIZE;

			local timedInteraction = false;
			interactionInterrupted = false;

			if interactionTime ~= nil then
				timedInteraction = true;
				timedInteractionDown = true;
				progressBar.Visible = true;
				progressBar.Size = newUDim2(0, 0, 1, 0);
				local initialT = tick();
				deltaT = 0

				while deltaT < interactionTime and (not interactionInterrupted) do
					game:GetService("RunService").Stepped:Wait()
					deltaT = tick() - initialT;
					local progress = deltaT / interactionTime;
					progressBar.Size = newUDim2(progress, 0, 1, 0);
					task.wait();
					if interactionInterrupted then
						--interactionInterrupted = false;
						break;
					end;
				end;
				deltaT = 0;
			end;
			if (timedInteraction and not interactionInterrupted) or (not timedInteraction) then
				timedInteractionDown = false;
				event(part);
--[[ 			elseif timedInteraction and interactionInterrupted then
				interactionInterrupted = false; ]]
			end;
		elseif inputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
			keyBtn.Size = KEY_BTN_DEFAULT_SIZE;
			if timedInteractionDown then
				interactionInterrupted = true;
				timedInteractionDown = false;
			end
			progressBar.Visible = false;
			progressBar.Size = newUDim2(0, 0, 1, 0);
		end;
	end, true);

	ContextActionUtility:SetTitle(uniqueIdentifier, name);

	self.InputBegan = inputBegan:Connect(function(input, onGUI)
		if onGUI then return; end;

		if input.KeyCode == key then
			keyBtn.Size = KEY_BTN_PRESSED_SIZE;

			local timedInteraction = false;
			interactionInterrupted = false;

			if interactionTime ~= nil then
				timedInteraction = true;
				timedInteractionDown = true;
				progressBar.Visible = true;
				progressBar.Size = newUDim2(0, 0, 1, 0);
				local initialT = tick();
				deltaT = 0

				while deltaT < interactionTime and (not interactionInterrupted) do
					game:GetService("RunService").Stepped:Wait()
					deltaT = tick() - initialT;
					local progress = deltaT / interactionTime;
					progressBar.Size = newUDim2(progress, 0, 1, 0);
					task.wait();
					if interactionInterrupted then
						--interactionInterrupted = false;
						break;
					end;
				end;
				deltaT = 0;
			end;
			if (timedInteraction and not interactionInterrupted) or (not timedInteraction) then
				timedInteractionDown = false;
				event(part);
--[[ 			elseif timedInteraction and interactionInterrupted then
				interactionInterrupted = false; ]]
			end;
		end;
	end);

	if not interactGUIEnabled then
		show:Play();
	end;
end;

function Interaction:Hide()
	local nameLabel = self.NameLabel;
	if not nameLabel then return; end;
	nameLabel:Destroy();
	self.NameLabel = nil;
	if #getChildren(interactGUI) == 2 then
		interactGUI.Enabled = false;
		interactGUI.Adornee = nil;
	end;

	local uniqueIdentifier = self.UniqueIdentifier;

	ContextActionUtility:UnbindAction(uniqueIdentifier);

	self.InputBegan:Disconnect();
	self.InputEnded:Disconnect();
end;

function Interaction:Start()
	interactGUI.ChildAdded:Connect(function()
		interactGUI.Size = newUDim2(0, 400, 0, 35 * (#getChildren(interactGUI) - 1));
	end);
	interactGUI.Parent = playerGUI;
end;

function Interaction:Init()
	Map = self.Shared.Map;
end;

return Interaction;
