local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local NetworkController;

local TAKE_AMMO_EVENT;

local Ammo = {};

local db = false

function Ammo.Get(interactionPart)
    if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then
        if Players.LocalPlayer.Team.Name ~= interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then return end
    end
    if (Players.LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - interactionPart.Position).Magnitude > 5 then return; end;
    return 'Take Ammo', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function Ammo.Event(ammoPart)
    if db then return end
    db = true
    NetworkController.Send(TAKE_AMMO_EVENT, ammoPart);
    task.wait(0.5)
    db = false
end;

function Ammo:Start()

end;

function Ammo:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Ammo;
    TAKE_AMMO_EVENT = constants.TAKE_AMMO_EVENT;
end;

return Ammo;

-- Book Players
-- Khizzer
-- June 21, 2021

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local BookPlayers = {};

local BookGUI
local Whitelist;

function BookPlayers.Get()
    local weld = localPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint')

    if not weld then return; end;
    if not Whitelist[localPlayer.Team.Name] then return; end;

    local suspectTorso = weld.Part0;
    local suspectChar = suspectTorso.Parent;

    local suspectPlr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectChar);
    if suspectPlr:GetAttribute('InZipties') then return; end;

    return 'Book Player', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 2;
end;

function BookPlayers.Event()
    if not BookGUI.IsEnabled() then
        BookGUI.Enable();
    else
        BookGUI.Disable();
    end;
end;

function BookPlayers:Start()
end

function BookPlayers:Init()
    BookGUI = self.Controllers.UI.BookGUI;
    Whitelist = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return BookPlayers

-- Purchase
-- Khizzer
-- April 6, 2023



local Purchase = {}

local MarketplaceService = game:GetService('MarketplaceService');

function Purchase.Get(interactionPart)
    return 'Purchase', Enum.KeyCode.F;
end;

function Purchase.Event(interactionPart)
    local shirt = interactionPart.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass('Shirt');
    local pants = interactionPart.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass('Pants');

    local shirtId;
    local pantsId;

    if shirt then
        shirtId = shirt:GetAttribute('ShirtId');
    end;

    if pants then
        pantsId = pants:GetAttribute('PantsId');
    end;

    MarketplaceService:PromptPurchase(game.Players.LocalPlayer, (shirtId or pantsId));
end;


return Purchase

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/BusinessPhone.lua ---

--[[
    BusinessPhone (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions
    Parent: Interactions
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Business Phone
-- Khizzer
-- March 1, 2024

local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkFunctionController;
local DeveloperCheck;

local BusinessPhone = {}

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local char;

function BusinessPhone.Get(interactionPart)
    if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then
        if localPlayer.Team.Name ~= interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then return; end;
    else
        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Authenticated') == nil then
            local group, rank = interactionPart:GetAttribute("GroupID"), interactionPart:GetAttribute("MinRank");

            interactionPart:SetAttribute('Authenticated', localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(group) >= rank or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer));
        end
        if not interactionPart:GetAttribute('Authenticated') then return end
    end

    return 'Answer Phone', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function BusinessPhone:CharacterAdded(_char)
    char = _char;
end

function BusinessPhone.Event(interactionPart)
    NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('CALL_PICKUP', interactionPart.Parent.Name);
    if localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Phone') then
        char.Humanoid:EquipTool(localPlayer.Backpack.Phone);
    end;
end

function BusinessPhone:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
end


return BusinessPhone

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/BusinessTool.lua ---

--[[
    BusinessTool (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions
    Parent: Interactions
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Business Tool
-- Khizzer
-- September 5, 2022



local BusinessTool = {}

local BusinessToolGUI;
local Authorisation;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

function BusinessTool.Get(interactionPart)
    local keycode = if interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(workspace.Cars) then Enum.KeyCode.M else Enum.KeyCode.E
    local cache = interactionPart:GetAttribute('CACHE_ALLOWED');
    if cache then
        if cache == false then
            return;
        elseif cache == true then
            return 'Tool Dispenser', keycode, if interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(workspace.Cars) then 0.5 else nil;
        end;
    end;

    local toolConfig = require(interactionPart.ToolConfig);

    local auth, doCache = Authorisation(localPlayer, toolConfig);
    if doCache then interactionPart:SetAttribute('CACHE_ALLOWED', auth) end;
    if not auth then return end;
    return 'Tool Dispenser', keycode, if interactionPart:IsDescendantOf(workspace.Cars) then 0.5 else nil;
end;

function BusinessTool.Event(interactionPart)
    local toolConfig = require(interactionPart.ToolConfig);

    BusinessToolGUI:Toggle(interactionPart, toolConfig.Tools);
end;

function BusinessTool:Init()
    Authorisation = self.Shared.Authorisation;
    BusinessToolGUI = self.Controllers.UI.BusinessToolGUI;
end;


return BusinessTool

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/BusinessUniform.lua ---

--[[
    BusinessUniform (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions
    Parent: Interactions
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Business Uniform
-- Khizzer
-- April 17, 2023



local BusinessUniform = {}

local NetworkController;
local DeveloperCheck;

type UniformConfig = {
    GroupID: number;
    MinimumRank: number;
};

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

function BusinessUniform.Get(interactionPart)
    local cache = interactionPart:GetAttribute('CACHE_ALLOWED');
    if cache then
        if cache == false then
            return;
        elseif cache == true then
            if localPlayer.Character:GetAttribute('HasBusinessUniform') then return 'Take Off Uniform', Enum.KeyCode.F; end;
            return 'Business Uniform', Enum.KeyCode.F;
        end;
    end;

    local uniformConfig: UniformConfig = require(interactionPart.UniformConfig);

    if DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) then
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('CACHE_ALLOWED', true);
        return;
    end;

    if localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(uniformConfig.GroupID) < uniformConfig.MinimumRank then
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('CACHE_ALLOWED', false);
        return;
    else
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('CACHE_ALLOWED', true);
        return;
    end;
end;

function BusinessUniform.Event(interactionPart)
    NetworkController.Send('BusinessUniform', interactionPart);
end;

function BusinessUniform:Init()
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return BusinessUniform

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/CarHitch.lua ---

--[[
    CarHitch (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions
    Parent: Interactions
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Car Hitch
-- Khizzer
-- January 22, 2023

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local car = localPlayer:WaitForChild('Car');

local NetworkController;

local CarHitch = {}

function CarHitch.Get(interactionPart)
    local trailerHinge = interactionPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("TrailerHinge");
    if not trailerHinge then return; end;

    if interactionPart.Parent.Parent.Parent ~= car.Value then return; end;

    local hingeAttachment0 = trailerHinge.Attachment0; --Check if its connected to a trailer
    if not hingeAttachment0 then
        return 'Attach Trailer', Enum.KeyCode.E;
    end;

    return 'Detach Trailer', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function CarHitch.Event(interactionPart)
    local trailerHinge = interactionPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("TrailerHinge");
    if not trailerHinge then return; end;

    local hingeAttachment0 = trailerHinge.Attachment0; 
    if not hingeAttachment0 then --Check if its connected to a trailer
        NetworkController.Send('TruckHitchBegin', interactionPart);
        return;
    end;
    
    NetworkController.Send('DetatchTrailer', interactionPart);

end;

function CarHitch:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return CarHitch

--[[
    Cartridges (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions
    Parent: Interactions
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local NetworkController;

local TAKE_CARTRIDGES_EVENT;

local Cartridges = {};

local db = false

function Cartridges.Get(interactionPart)
    if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then
        if Players.LocalPlayer.Team.Name ~= interactionPart:GetAttribute('Team') then return end
    end
    if (Players.LocalPlayer.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - interactionPart.Position).Magnitude > 5 then return; end;
    return 'Take Cartridges', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function Cartridges.Event(cartridgesPart)
    if db then return end
    db = true
    NetworkController.Send(TAKE_CARTRIDGES_EVENT, cartridgesPart);
    task.wait(0.5)
    db = false
end;

function Cartridges:Start()

end;

function Cartridges:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Cartridges;
    TAKE_CARTRIDGES_EVENT = constants.TAKE_CARTRIDGES_EVENT;
end;

return Cartridges;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/Door.lua ---

--[[
    Door (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions
    Parent: Interactions
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local NetworkController;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local Door = {};

function Door.Get(doorInteractionPart)
    local doorConfig = require(doorInteractionPart.Parent.DoorConfig);
    if localPlayer:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
    if (localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1) then return; end;

    if doorConfig.SpecialCondition then
        if doorConfig.SpecialCondition(localPlayer) then
            if localPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
                return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 2;
            end;
            return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E;
        end
        if not doorConfig.GroupCondition and not doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams then return end
    end

    if doorConfig.GroupCondition then
		local cachedResult = doorInteractionPart:FindFirstChild('_CACHE');
        if not cachedResult then
            cachedResult = Instance.new('BoolValue');
            cachedResult.Name = '_CACHE';
            cachedResult.Value = doorConfig.GroupCondition(localPlayer);
            cachedResult.Parent = doorInteractionPart;
        end;
		if cachedResult.Value == true then
            if localPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
                return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 2;
            end;
            return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E;
        end;
        if cachedResult.Value == false and not doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams then return; end;
	end;

    if doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams then
        if localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil then
            if doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams[localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division')] then
                if localPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
                    return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 2;
                end;

                return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E;
            end;
        end;

        if not doorConfig.WhitelistedTeams[localPlayer.Team.Name] then return; end;
    end

    if localPlayer.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
        return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 2;
    end;

    return 'Open/Close', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function Door.Event(doorInteractionPart)
    NetworkController.Send('Door', doorInteractionPart);
end;

function Door:Start()

end;

function Door:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return Door;

local DuffelBag = {}

local backpack = localPlayer.Backpack;
local character = localPlayer.Character;

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

DuffelBag.Priority = 2

function DuffelBag:CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;
    backpack = localPlayer:WaitForChild('Backpack');
    character = char;
end;

function DuffelBag.Get(interactionPart)
--[[     local vector, onScreen = camera:WorldToScreenPoint(interactionPart.Position);
    if not onScreen then return; end; ]]
    if not backpack or not character then warn('No backpack or character found. Duffel bag interaction not shown.') return; end;

    if backpack:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag') then return; end;
    if character:FindFirstChild('Duffel Bag') then return; end;

    return 'Duffel Bag', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

    NetworkController.Send('GET_DUFFEL_BAG', interactionPart);

-- Fire Pole
-- Khizzer
-- March 29, 2022



local FirePole = {}

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local ModelAnimation;

function FirePole.Get()
    if localPlayer.Team.Name ~= 'Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service' then return; end;

    return 'Slide Down', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function FirePole.Event(part)
    local START_PART = part.Parent.Start;
    local END_PART = part.Parent.End;
    localPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(START_PART.CFrame);

    local animation = Instance.new('Animation');
    animation.AnimationId = 'rbxassetid://9228259462';

    local track = localPlayer.Character.Humanoid:WaitForChild('Animator'):LoadAnimation(animation)
    track:Play();
    local tween = ModelAnimation.new(localPlayer.Character, TweenInfo.new(), END_PART.CFrame, function()
        track:Stop();
    end);
    tween:Play();
end;

function FirePole:Init()
    ModelAnimation = self.Modules.ModelAnimation;
end;


return FirePole

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Gas Pump
-- Khizzer
-- July 26, 2021


local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local GasPumpGUI;

local GasPump = {}

function GasPump.Get(interactionPart: Part)
    if localPlayer.Car.Value == nil then return; end;
    if ((interactionPart.Position) - (localPlayer.Car.Value.Chassis.Mass.Position :: Vector3)).Magnitude > 30 then return; end;

    return 'Pump Gas', Enum.KeyCode.E;
end;

function GasPump.Event(interactionPart)
    GasPumpGUI:Enable(interactionPart);
end;

function GasPump:Init()
    GasPumpGUI = self.Controllers.UI.GasPumpGUI;
end;


return GasPump;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/Citation.lua ---

--[[
    Citation (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Citation
-- oSudden
-- 2021

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local NetworkController;

local CitationUI;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

local whitelistedTeams;

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
	if not char_ then return; end;
	char = char_;
	rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local Citation = {};

function Citation.Get(suspectRootPart)
	if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
		CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
		return;
	end;

	if not char:FindFirstChild('Citation') then return; end;

	local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
	if not plr then return; end;
	if whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;
	if suspectRootPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and suspectRootPart.Parent.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

	return 'Add citation', Enum.KeyCode.X
end;

function Citation.Event(suspectRootPart)
	CitationUI:Enable(game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent))
end;

function Citation:Start()
	CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
	localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function Citation:Init()
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

	CitationUI = self.Controllers.UI.CitationGUI;

	local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;

	whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return Citation;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/Frisk.lua ---

--[[
    Frisk (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Frisk
-- Khizzer
-- June 23, 2022



-- Grab
-- Khizzer
-- June 14, 2021

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local FriskGUI;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

local whitelistedTeams;

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;
    char = char_;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local UNDERCOVERS = {"GCPS"};

local Frisk = {};

function Frisk.Get(suspectRootPart)
    if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        return;
    end;

    if not char:FindFirstChild('Handcuffs') and not char:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;
    if localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not whitelistedTeams[localPlayer.Team.Name] then return; end;

    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
    if not plr then return; end;
    if not plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
    if plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') and plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= localPlayer.Name then return; end;
    --if someone else grabbed, hide interaction
    if suspectRootPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and suspectRootPart.Parent.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

    if (plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy')) and (plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy')) then
        if plr.Team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') == 'CFNIS' then return 'Frisk', Enum.KeyCode.C; end;
        if whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and not table.find(UNDERCOVERS, localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h') and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;

        return 'Frisk', Enum.KeyCode.C
    end;
end;

function Frisk.Event(suspectRootPart)
    FriskGUI:Enable(Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent));
end;

function Frisk:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function Frisk:Init()

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;

    FriskGUI = self.Controllers.UI.FriskGUI;

    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return Frisk;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/Grab.lua ---

--[[
    Grab (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Grab
-- Khizzer
-- June 14, 2021

local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local NetworkController;

local GRAB_EVENT;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

local whitelistedTeams;

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;
    char = char_;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local Grab = {};

function Grab.Get(suspectRootPart)
    if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        return;
    end;

    if not char:FindFirstChild('Handcuffs') then return; end;

    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
    if not plr then return; end;
    if not plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
    if plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') and plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= localPlayer.Name then return; end;
    --if someone else grabbed, hide interaction
    if suspectRootPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and suspectRootPart.Parent.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

    if (plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy')) and (not plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy')) then
        if plr.Team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' and (localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') == 'CFNIS' or localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") == '1MPR') then return 'Grab', Enum.KeyCode.E; end;
        if whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;

        if plr:GetAttribute("Protectee") and (localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h'):sub(1,3) == "POU" then
            return 'Grab', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 3
        end

        return 'Grab', Enum.KeyCode.E
    end;
end;

function Grab.Event(suspectRootPart)
    NetworkController.Send(GRAB_EVENT, suspectRootPart);
end;

function Grab:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function Grab:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;
    GRAB_EVENT = constants.GRAB_EVENT;

    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return Grab;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/GrabZiptie.lua ---

--[[
    GrabZiptie (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Grab Ziptie
-- Khizzer
-- November 24, 2023



local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local NetworkController;

local Whitelist;
local whitelistedTeams;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;
    char = char_;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local Grab = {};

function Grab.Get(suspectRootPart)
    if not Whitelist[localPlayer.Team.Name] and not Whitelist[localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division')] then return; end;

    if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        return;
    end;

    if not char:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;
    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
    if not plr then return; end;
    if not plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
    if plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') and plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= localPlayer.Name then return; end;
    if localPlayer.Team.Name == "Civilian" and not plr:GetAttribute('InZipties') and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then return; end;
    if suspectRootPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and suspectRootPart.Parent.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;
    if whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return end

    if (plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy')) and (not plr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy')) then
        return 'Grab', Enum.KeyCode.E
    end;
end;

function Grab.Event(suspectRootPart)
    NetworkController.Send('ZiptieGrab', suspectRootPart);
end;

function Grab:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function Grab:Init()
    Whitelist = self.Shared.Constants.Ziptie.Whitelist;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;
    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return Grab;



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/Handcuff.lua ---

--[[
    Handcuff (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local NetworkController;

local HANDCUFF_EVENT;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;
local InteractionController;

local whitelistedTeams;

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;
    char = char_;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local Handcuff = {};

function Handcuff.Get(suspectRootPart)
    if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        return;
    end;

    if not char:FindFirstChild('Handcuffs') then return; end;
    if not whitelistedTeams[localPlayer.Team.Name] then return; end;

    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
    if not plr then return; end;--    if InteractionController:GetClosestPart(suspectRootPart) then return; end;

    if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;

    if plr.Team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' and (localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') == 'CFNIS' or localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") == "1MPR") then return 'Handcuff', Enum.KeyCode.E, 0.5; end;
    if whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;
    if suspectRootPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and suspectRootPart.Parent.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

    if
        ((localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") or 'h'):sub(1,3) == "POU" and plr:GetAttribute("Protectee"))
        or plr:FindFirstChild("respawningValue") or plr:GetAttribute("Releasing")
    then
        return 'Handcuff', Enum.KeyCode.E, nil, 3
    end

    return 'Handcuff', Enum.KeyCode.E, 0.5;
end;

function Handcuff.Event(suspectRootPart)
    NetworkController.Send(HANDCUFF_EVENT, suspectRootPart);
end;

function Handcuff:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function Handcuff:Init()
    InteractionController = self.Controllers.InteractionController;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;
    HANDCUFF_EVENT = constants.HANDCUFF_EVENT;

    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return Handcuff;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/RemoveZiptie.lua ---

--[[
    RemoveZiptie (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Remove Ziptie
-- Khizzer
-- November 9, 2023

local Players = game:GetService("Players")


local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local NetworkController;
local Whitelist;
local whitelistedTeams;

local char;

local RemoveZiptie = {}

function RemoveZiptie.Get(interactionPart)
    if not Whitelist[localPlayer.Team.Name] and not Whitelist[localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division')] then return; end;
    if not char:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;

    local targetChar = interactionPart.Parent;

    local targetPlr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(targetChar);
    if not targetPlr then return; end;
    if localPlayer.Team.Name == "Civilian" and not targetPlr:GetAttribute('InZipties') and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;
    if whitelistedTeams[targetPlr.Team.Name] and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then return end

    if targetPlr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') ~= localPlayer.Name then return; end;

    return 'Remove Zipcuffs', Enum.KeyCode.V;
end

function RemoveZiptie.Event(interactionPart)
   NetworkController.Send('ZiptieRestrain', interactionPart);
end

function RemoveZiptie:CharacterAdded(_char)
    char = _char;
end

function RemoveZiptie:Init()
    Whitelist = self.Shared.Constants.Ziptie.Whitelist;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;
    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;


return RemoveZiptie

local NetworkController;

local HANDCUFF_EVENT;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

local whitelistedTeams;

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;
    char = char_;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local RemoveHandcuff = {};

function RemoveHandcuff.Get(suspectRootPart)
    if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        return;
    end;

    if not char:FindFirstChild('Handcuffs') then return; end;

    local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
    if not plr then return; end;
    if plr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') ~= localPlayer.Name then return; end;

    if plr.Team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' and (localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') == 'CFNIS' or localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") == '1MPR') then return 'Remove Handcuffs', Enum.KeyCode.V; end;
    if whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;
    return 'Remove Handcuffs', Enum.KeyCode.V
end;

function RemoveHandcuff.Event(suspectRootPart)
    NetworkController.Send(HANDCUFF_EVENT, suspectRootPart);
end;

function RemoveHandcuff:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function RemoveHandcuff:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;
    HANDCUFF_EVENT = constants.HANDCUFF_EVENT;

    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return RemoveHandcuff;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/SearchBody.lua ---

--[[
    SearchBody (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local FriskGUI;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

local whitelistedTeams;

local UNDERCOVERS = {"GCPS"};

local function CharacterAdded(char_)
    if not char_ then return; end;
    char = char_;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local SearchBody = {};

local FEATURE_ENABLED = false

function SearchBody.Get(suspectRootPart)
    if not FEATURE_ENABLED then
        return
    end
    if suspectRootPart == rootPart then
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
        return;
    end;

    if not localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Handcuffs') and localPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;
    if localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not whitelistedTeams[localPlayer.Team.Name] then return; end;
    local human = suspectRootPart.Parent:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
    if not human then return end
    if human.Health > 1 then return end
    -- local plr = Players[suspectRootPart.Parent.Name];
    -- local isChar = plr and (plr.Character == suspectRootPart.Parent)
    -- if the team name isn't known we treat them like a cop just to be safe
    local teamName = human:GetAttribute('PlayerTeam') or 'Vancouver Police Department'

    if teamName == 'Canadian Armed Forces' and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') == 'CFNIS' then return 'Search body', Enum.KeyCode.C, 2; end;
    if whitelistedTeams[teamName] and localPlayer:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;

    return 'Search body', Enum.KeyCode.C, 2
end;

function SearchBody.Event(suspectRootPart)
    print('Search body', suspectRootPart.Parent:GetAttribute('GUID'))
    -- FriskGUI:Enable(Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent));
end;

function SearchBody:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function SearchBody:Init()
    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;

    FriskGUI = self.Controllers.UI.FriskGUI;

    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return SearchBody;



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Interactions/HumanoidRootPart/Ziptie.lua ---

--[[
    Ziptie (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Interactions → HumanoidRootPart
    Parent: HumanoidRootPart
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Ziptie
-- Khizzer
-- November 5, 2023

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")


local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local NetworkController;
local Whitelist;
local whitelistedTeams;

local char;

local Ziptie = {}

function Ziptie.Get(interactionPart)
    if not Whitelist[localPlayer.Team.Name] and not Whitelist[localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division')] then return; end;
    if not char:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;

    local targetChar = interactionPart.Parent;

    local targetPlr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(targetChar);
    if not targetPlr then return; end;

    if whitelistedTeams[targetPlr.Team.Name] and localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(localPlayer) then return; end;
    if targetPlr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then return; end;
    if targetChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and targetChar.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

    return 'Restrain', Enum.KeyCode.E, 0.5;
end

function Ziptie.Event(interactionPart)
    NetworkController.Send('ZiptieRestrain', interactionPart);
end

function Ziptie:CharacterAdded(_char)
    char = _char;
end

function Ziptie:Init()
    Whitelist = self.Shared.Constants.Ziptie.Whitelist;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    whitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff.WhitelistedTeams;
end;


return Ziptie

local plr = Players.LocalPlayer

local Warp = {}

function Warp.Get(p)
  if plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return end
  if p:GetAttribute("Location") == "BCSS" then return end
  return 'BCSS (SZ)', Enum.KeyCode.B, 1.5
end

  NetworkController.Send('intelWarps/GoTo', 'BCSS')
end

end
